< review>
I have a 2008, 535 with 75k miles.
I had the car serviced at the local dealer while it was under warranty, but that is now over.
I had a 'check engine' light on and brought it to the dealer. They thought they diagnosed it and changed a part, but that did not work so they put my old part back in (but did not charge me for this, other than the diagnosis fee).
They said the repair needed now is a carbon cleaning ($800) and replace the fuel injector. They also said they cannot replace one injector, but instead have to replace all of them even if only one is causing a problem, and this was going to be $2200.
Instead, I brought the car to Hal, at Bavarian Performance, and he did their carbon cleaning for half the dealer price. Hal also was skeptical of the need for injectors so certainly suggested not replacing those.
Result?  The car is running sweet again!
My car will be going back to Hal, when something is needed.<//review>

I found him to not only to be extremely knowledgeable, but also very professional.  He knows BMWs and knows how to treat people, whether they are customers or employees.  In the end he fixed my car without issue and in short order.  I will be back.  Finding an honest, knowledgeable and professional mechanic is not an easy task.  I highly recommend this shop to anyone with a BMW that is looking for an independent shop.< /text>

<date>1512591844120< /date><review>Great, intimate space to do work. The coffee shop is small and located inside a converted train car, so it's not great for groups, but perfect for working alone or with a partner. There is always great music playing and local art displayed and for sale. Everyone's super chill and seems happy to be there.

The Aztec mocha is fantastic, and I recommend it blended.

PROS:
--Good selection of drinks with some space-specfic specialties
--Lots of natural lighting
--Showcases local artists on a rotating basis;  can purchase the art
--Small enough place that you can develop a good relationship with the baristas if you come regularly enough
--Board games

CONS:
--They use sweetened condensed milk in their blended drinks, which I hadn't been told about as I had been ordering mine with soy. Luckily I don't have an allergy, but make sure to ask for it without it.
--Limited seating. It's a small space, and the train car seating, while in theme, can be limiting if one person takes a table for 4. I've heard of people asking to share when crowded
--You can feel the place shake. Probably not noticeable for most, but if you're sensitive to motions, it is there
--There's a constant whirring of the AC/heating unit. Again, if you're not sensitive to noise, you probably won't notice it, but it drives me crazy<//review><UserId.>111176201251067190462</UserId.></record></dataset><record>
